<p>We have a small team of experts working in the engineering team and your role is responsible for the execution of plant investment projects to the agreed scope, quality and schedule. Instrumentation engineering in our projects includes all project phases from idea creation, pre-study and feasibility study via basic engineering to detailed engineering and As Built phase. In addition, our instrument engineers are also involved in pre-commissioning, commissioning and start-up phases<\u002Fp> \n     <ul>\n      <li>Perform design tasks according to the agreed quality, scope, time and safety<\u002Fli> \n      <li>Develop, implement and apply NES defined design engineering work methods and tools systematically<\u002Fli> \n      <li>Manage own performance, and the performance of the work share partners<\u002Fli> \n      <li>Develop oneself in leading design work and workshare partners, or towards becoming a design specialist of own engineering discipline<\u002Fli> \n      <li>Collaborate and network with other design disciplines, workshare partners, suppliers and customers<\u002Fli> \n      <li>Participate in bid preparation, execution planning and cost estimates<\u002Fli> \n      <li>Take part in developing our instructions and way of working<\u002Fli> \n      <li>Provide engineering support in resolving site queries and site issues<\u002Fli> \n      <li>Participate as construction supervisor for instrumentation works at site during turnarounds and shutdowns<\u002Fli> \n     <\u002Ful> \n     <p>In this role you will report to the Engineering Team Manager.
